***whiting.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:whiting.html>whiting</a> (78044)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Latn mention" lang="en">white</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">-ing</i>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:whiting.html>whiting</a></strong> (<i>usually uncountable</i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">whitings</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A fine white chalk used in paints, putty, whitewash etc.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">whitening</span></span></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms hyponym"><span class="defdate">Hyponyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">French white</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">Paris white</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">Spanish white</span></span></dd></dl>
<ul><li><b>1918</b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:hannah.html>Hannah</a> Teresa Rowley, ‎Mrs. <a href = vnd.unilang:helen.html>Helen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:louise.html>Louise</a> (Wales) Farrell, <i>Principles of Chemistry Applied to the Household</i>
<dl><dd>Precipitated calcium carbonate, a very fine powdery form, <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> used as a basis for many tooth powders and pastes. As <b><a href = vnd.unilang:whiting.html>whiting</a></b> it finds a wide use in cleaning metals of their tarnishes.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:whiting.html>whiting</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">present participle of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Latn mention" lang="en">white</i></span></span></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:242px;"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/40/Merlangius_merlangus.jpg/240px-Merlangius_merlangus.jpg" decoding="async" width="240" height="89" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/40/Merlangius_merlangus.jpg/360px-Merlangius_merlangus.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/40/Merlangius_merlangus.jpg/480px-Merlangius_merlangus.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1190" data-file-height="440" />  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"></div>a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:whiting.html>whiting</a></b> (<i>Merlangius merlangus</i>)</div></div></div>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">whityng</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">whytyng</i>, perhaps an alteration of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">hwītling</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:whiting.html>whiting</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, remodelled after <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">white</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">-ing</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="ann-pos">diminutive <a href = vnd.unilang:suffix.html>suffix</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Related to the colour white. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">wijting</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:whiting.html>whiting</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse">Old <a href = vnd.unilang:norse.html>Norse</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">hvítingr</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">a <a href = vnd.unilang:kind.html>kind</a> of whale</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:whiting.html>whiting</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">whitings</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:whiting.html>whiting</a></strong></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A fish, <i>Merlangius merlangus</i>, similar to cod, found in the North Atlantic; <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_whiting" class="extiw" title="w:English whiting">English <a href = vnd.unilang:whiting.html>whiting</a></a> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">US</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>.</li>
<li>Any fish of many species that resemble <i>Merlangius merlangus</i>:
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/United_States" class="extiw" title="w:United States">US</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Any of several marine fish found in North American coastal waters, including hakes (genus <i>Merluccius</i>), especially <span class="biota"><a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Merluccius_bilinearis" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Merluccius bilinearis"><i>Merluccius bilinearis</i></a></span> (the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/silver_hake" class="extiw" title="w:silver hake">silver <a href = vnd.unilang:haken.html>hake</a></a>).</li>
<li>Any of the species of <span class="biota"><a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Sillaginidae" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Sillaginidae">Sillaginidae</a></span> (<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/smelt-whiting" class="extiw" title="w:smelt-whiting">smelt-whitings</a>) inhabiting Indo-Pacific marine coasts, many of which are commercially important whitefish.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Canada" class="extiw" title="w:Canada">Canada</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Alaska pollock (<i>Gadus chalcogrammus</i>, syn. <i>Theragra chalcogramma</i>).</li>
<li>A blue <a href = vnd.unilang:whiting.html>whiting</a> (<span class="biota"><a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Micromesistius_poutassou" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Micromesistius poutassou"><i>Micromesistius poutassou</i></a></span>), a marine fish of the Northern Hemisphere.</li>
<li>A <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/southern_blue_whiting" class="extiw" title="w:southern blue whiting">southern blue <a href = vnd.unilang:whiting.html>whiting</a></a> (<span class="biota"><a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Micromesistius_australis" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Micromesistius australis"><i>Micromesistius australis</i></a></span>), a marine fish of the Southern Hemisphere.</li>
<li><span class="biota"><a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Menticirrhus_americanus" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Menticirrhus americanus"><i>Menticirrhus americanus</i></a></span> (<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Carolina_whiting" class="extiw" title="w:Carolina whiting">Carolina <a href = vnd.unilang:whiting.html>whiting</a></a>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/king_whiting" class="extiw" title="w:king whiting">king <a href = vnd.unilang:whiting.html>whiting</a></a>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/southern_kingcroaker" class="extiw" title="w:southern kingcroaker">southern kingcroaker</a>, and <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/southern_kingfish" class="extiw" title="w:southern kingfish">southern kingfish</a>) found along the Atlantic and Gulf Coasts of the United States.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/India" class="extiw" title="w:India">India</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Australia" class="extiw" title="w:Australia">Australia</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Any of the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/smelt-whiting" class="extiw" title="w:smelt-whiting">smelt-whitings</a>, of the family <span class="biota"><a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Sillaginidae" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Sillaginidae">Sillaginidae</a></span>, including <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Japanese_whiting" class="extiw" title="w:Japanese whiting">Japanese <a href = vnd.unilang:whiting.html>whiting</a></a>, King George <a href = vnd.unilang:whiting.html>whiting</a>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/northern_whiting" class="extiw" title="w:northern whiting">northern <a href = vnd.unilang:whiting.html>whiting</a></a>, sand <a href = vnd.unilang:whiting.html>whiting</a>, and <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/school_whiting" class="extiw" title="w:school whiting">school <a href = vnd.unilang:whiting.html>whiting</a></a>.</li></ol></li></ol>
</body>

***whoosh.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:whoosh.html>whoosh</a> (62241)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:whoosh.html>whoosh</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">whooshes</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A breathy sound like that of an object passing at high speed.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2012</b>,  John Branch,  “Snow Fall : The Avalanche at <a href = vnd.unilang:tunnel.html>Tunnel</a> Creek”, in  <cite>New York Time</cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://www.nytimes.com/projects/2012/snow-fall/?smid=fb-nytimesamp;WT.z_sma=SP_SNT_20130415/?part=tunnel-creek">[1]</a></sup>:</span><dl><dd></dd></dl></div>
<dl><dd>The snow burst through the trees with no warning but a last-second <b><a href = vnd.unilang:whoosh.html>whoosh</a></b> of sound, a two-story wall of white and Chris Rudolph’s piercing cry: “Avalanche! Elyse!”</dd></dl></li>
<li>"I love <a href = vnd.unilang:deadlines.html>deadlines</a>. I like the <b>whooshing</b> sound they make as they fly by." —Douglas Adams</li></ul></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:whoosh.html>whoosh</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">whooshes</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">whooshing</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">whooshed</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>To make a breathy sound like a <a href = vnd.unilang:whoosh.html>whoosh</a>.</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Interjection">Interjection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:whoosh.html>whoosh</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">sarcastic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="use-with-mention">Indicating that somebody <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> missed the point (i.e. it <a href = vnd.unilang:went.html>went</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a> their head).</span></li></ol>
</body>

<p><i class="Latn mention" lang="en">whop</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:dictatoriaal.html>-er</a></i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:whopper.html>whopper</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:whoppers.html>whoppers</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">informal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Something remarkably large.
<ul><li><b>1939</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Noel_Langley" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Noel Langley">Noel <a href = vnd.unilang:langley.html>Langley</a></a>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Florence_Ryerson" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Florence Ryerson">Florence Ryerson</a>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Edgar_Allan_Woolf" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Edgar Allan Woolf"><a href = vnd.unilang:edgar.html>Edgar</a> Allan Woolf</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Wizard_of_Oz_(1939_film)" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:The Wizard of Oz (1939 film)">The Wizard of <a href = vnd.unilang:oz.html>Oz</a></a></i>
<dl><dd>There's a <a href = vnd.unilang:storm.html>storm</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:blowing.html>blowing</a> up, <a href = vnd.unilang:sylvester.html>Sylvester</a>  |  a '<b><a href = vnd.unilang:whopper.html>whopper</a>'</b>, speaking in the vernacular of the peasantry.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">informal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> An outrageous or blatant lie.</li></ol>
</body>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> why (210)</h1><br><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Bijwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:bijwoord.html>Bijwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b>why</b>
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:waarom.html>waarom</a>
<dl><dd>«<b>Why</b> have you done this?»
<dl><dd><i><b><a href = vnd.unilang:waarom.html>Waarom</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:heb.html>heb</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dit.html>dit</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gedaan.html>gedaan</a>?</i></dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Voegwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:voegwoord.html>Voegwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b>why</b>
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:waarom.html>waarom</a>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:wicht.html>wicht</a> (13603)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:wicht.html>wicht</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">wiht</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*wihtą</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:wight.html>wight</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:wicht.html>Wicht</a></i>.

***wick.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:wick.html>wick</a> (24320)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href = vnd.unilang:weke.html>weke</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">wicke</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:wick.html>wick</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">wēoce</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:wick.html>wick</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*weukan</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">flax bundle, <a href = vnd.unilang:wick.html>wick</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*weg-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to weave</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup> Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">wjok</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">wjuk</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">wing</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wiek.html>wiek</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">wing; propeller, blade; <a href = vnd.unilang:wick.html>wick</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Wieche</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">wisp; <a href = vnd.unilang:wick.html>wick</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:wick.html>wick</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:wicks.html>wicks</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A bundle, twist, braid, or woven strip of cord, fabric, fibre/fiber, or other porous material in a candle, oil <a href = vnd.unilang:lamp.html>lamp</a>, kerosene heater, or the like, that draws up liquid fuel, such as melted tallow, wax, or the oil, delivering it to the base of the flame for conversion to gases and burning; any other length of material burned for illumination in small successive portions.
<dl><dd><i>Trim the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:wick.html>wick</a></b> fairly short, so that the flame does not smoke.</i></dd></dl>
<ul><li><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(Can <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> date this quote by Edmund Spenser and provide title, author’s full name, and other <a href = vnd.unilang:details.html>details</a>?)</span>
<dl><dd>But true it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a>, that when the oil <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> spent / The light goes out, and <b><a href = vnd.unilang:wick.html>wick</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> thrown away.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li>Any piece of porous material that conveys liquid by capillary action, such as a strip of gauze placed in a wound to serve as a drain.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">curling</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A narrow opening in the field, flanked by other players' stones.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">curling</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A shot where the played stone touches a stationary stone just enough that the played stone changes direction.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> euphemistic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The <a href = vnd.unilang:penis.html>penis</a>.
<ul><li><b>2008</b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:marcus.html>Marcus</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>Van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:heller.html>Heller</a>, <i>Nest of Vixens</i>, →ISBN, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://books.google.ca/books?id=CG7a6LBMs4kCamp;dq=%22his+wick%22+%22stone+stiff%22amp;q=%22His+wick+was+stone+stiff%22v=snippetamp;q=%22His%20wick%20was%20stone%20stiff%22amp;f=false">p. 17</a>:
<dl><dd>His <b><a href = vnd.unilang:wick.html>wick</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> stone stiff.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>2009</b>, Ira Robbins, <i>Kick It Till It <a href = vnd.unilang:breaks.html>Breaks</a></i>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Trouser_Press" class="extiw" title="w:Trouser Press">Trouser Press</a>, →ISBN, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://books.google.ca/books?id=j5vOrRdUG4wCamp;dq=sucked+%22his+wick%22+subject%3A%22fiction%22amp;q=%22his+wick%22v=snippetamp;q=%22his%20wick%22amp;f=false">p. 130</a>:
<dl><dd>Her laugh wasn'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> cruel in tone, but it cut through Husk like a <a href = vnd.unilang:scalpel.html>scalpel</a>, withering his <b><a href = vnd.unilang:wick.html>wick</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:even.html>even</a> further.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:wick.html>wick</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:wicks.html>wicks</a></b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">wicking</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">wicked</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To convey or draw off (liquid) by capillary action.
<dl><dd><i>The fabric <b><a href = vnd.unilang:wicks.html>wicks</a></b> perspiration away from the body.</i></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> of a liquid</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To traverse (i.e. be conveyed by capillary action) through a <a href = vnd.unilang:wick.html>wick</a> or other porous material, as water through a sponge. Usually followed by <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">through</i>.
<dl><dd><i>The moisture slowly <b>wicked</b> through the wood.</i></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">curling</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To strike (a stone) obliquely; to strike (a stationary stone) just enough that the played stone changes direction.</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From earlier <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href = vnd.unilang:wik.html>wik</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">wich</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">village, <a href = vnd.unilang:hamlet.html>hamlet</a>, town</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">wīc</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">dwelling place, abode</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; Germanic borrowing from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">vīcus</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">village, estate</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (see <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">vicinity</i>). It <a href = vnd.unilang:came.html>came</a> to mean “dairy farm” around the 13th or 14th century; for instance, <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">Gatwick</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">Goat-farm</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognates include <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">wîch</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">wih</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">village</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Weichbild</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">municipal area</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wijk.html>wijk</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">quarter, district</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Frisian" class="extiw" title="w:Old Frisian">Old Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="ofs"><a href = vnd.unilang:wik.html>wik</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Saxon" class="extiw" title="w:Old Saxon">Old Saxon</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="osx">wic</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">village</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, as well as <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">οἶκος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">oîkos</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">house</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, whence English <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">eco-</i>. Doublet of <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">vicus</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:wick.html>wick</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:wicks.html>wicks</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li class="senseid" id="English-village"> <span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(Can <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> clean up<sup class="plainlinks">(<a class="external text" href="https://en.wiktionary.org/w/index.php?title=Wiktionary:Requests_for_cleanupamp;action=editamp;section=newamp;preloadtitle=%5B%5Bwick%5D%5D">+</a>)</sup> this sense?)</span> <span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A village; <a href = vnd.unilang:hamlet.html>hamlet</a>; castle; dwelling; street; creek; bay; harbour; a place of work, jurisdiction, or exercise of authority.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Great_Britain" class="extiw" title="w:Great Britain">Britain</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> dialect<span class="ib-comma">,</span> chiefly <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/East_Anglia" class="extiw" title="w:East Anglia">East Anglia</a> and <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Essex" class="extiw" title="w:Essex">Essex</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A farm, especially a dairy farm.</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li>Present in compounds (meaning “village”, “jurisdiction”, or “harbour”), as <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">-wick</i>, such as bailiwick, sheriffwick, Warwick, Greenwick, Gatwick, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Southwick,_Hampshire" class="extiw" title="w:Southwick, Hampshire">Southwick</a>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">Hampton <a href = vnd.unilang:wick.html>Wick</a></span> etc., also <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">-wich</i>.</li></ul>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">vicinity</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:villa.html>villa</a></span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">village</span></li>

<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">-wick</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology 3</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">cwic</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">alive</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; similar to an archaic meaning of <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">quick</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">endowed with life; having a high degree of vigor, energy, or activity</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, and <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">quicken</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">come to life</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:wick.html>wick</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en comparative-form-of" lang="en">wicker</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en comparative-form-of" lang="en">more <a href = vnd.unilang:wick.html>wick</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en superlative-form-of" lang="en">wickest</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en superlative-form-of" lang="en">most <a href = vnd.unilang:wick.html>wick</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Great_Britain" class="extiw" title="w:Great Britain">Britain</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> dialect<span class="ib-comma">,</span> derogatory<span class="ib-comma">,</span> chiefly <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Yorkshire" class="extiw" title="w:Yorkshire">Yorkshire</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Alive; lively; full of life; active; bustling; nimble; quick.
<dl><dd><i>as <b><a href = vnd.unilang:wick.html>wick</a></b> as an eel</i></dd>
<dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>T</a>' <b>wickest</b> young chap at ivver <a href = vnd.unilang:ah.html>Ah</a> seen.</i></dd>
<dd><i>He's a strange <b><a href = vnd.unilang:wick.html>wick</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:bairn.html>bairn</a> alus runnin' aboot.</i></dd>
<dd><i>I'<a href = vnd.unilang:ll.html>ll</a> skin ye <b><a href = vnd.unilang:wick.html>wick</a></b>!</i> (skin you alive)</dd>
<dd><i>I thowt they <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> dead last back end but they're <b><a href = vnd.unilang:wick.html>wick</a></b> enif noo.</i></dd>
<dd><i>"Are you afraid of going across the churchyard in the dark?" "<a href = vnd.unilang:lor.html>Lor</a>' bless yer noä miss! It isn'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> dead <a href = vnd.unilang:uns.html>uns</a> I'm scar'd on, it's <b><a href = vnd.unilang:wick.html>wick</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:uns.html>uns</a>."</i></dd>
<dd><i>I'<a href = vnd.unilang:ll.html>ll</a> swop wi' him my poor dead horse for his <b><a href = vnd.unilang:wick.html>wick</a></b>.</i> — <i>Ballads and <a href = vnd.unilang:songs.html>Songs</a> of the Peasantry of England</i>, page 210</dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Great_Britain" class="extiw" title="w:Great Britain">Britain</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> dialect<span class="ib-comma">,</span> derogatory<span class="ib-comma">,</span> chiefly Yorkshire</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> (Of inanimate <a href = vnd.unilang:objects.html>objects</a>) resistant to being put to use, stiff, stubborn (as for example a rope or a screw).</li></ol>

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:wick.html>wick</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Great_Britain" class="extiw" title="w:Great Britain">Britain</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> dialect<span class="ib-comma">,</span> chiefly <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Yorkshire" class="extiw" title="w:Yorkshire">Yorkshire</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Liveliness; life.
<dl><dd><i>I niver <a href = vnd.unilang:knew.html>knew</a> such an a thing afore in all my <b><a href = vnd.unilang:wick.html>wick</a></b>.</i> — Ashby, 12 July 1875</dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Great_Britain" class="extiw" title="w:Great Britain">Britain</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> dialect<span class="ib-comma">,</span> chiefly <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Yorkshire" class="extiw" title="w:Yorkshire">Yorkshire</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The growing part of a plant nearest to the roots.
<dl><dd><i>Fed close? Why, it's eaten into <a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a>' hard <b><a href = vnd.unilang:wick.html>wick</a></b>.</i> (<a href = vnd.unilang:spoken.html>spoken</a> of a pasture which <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> fed very close)</dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Great_Britain" class="extiw" title="w:Great Britain">Britain</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> dialect<span class="ib-comma">,</span> chiefly <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Yorkshire" class="extiw" title="w:Yorkshire">Yorkshire</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> horticulture</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span>  (Usually plural) The parts of weed roots that remain viable in the ground after inadequate digging prior to cultivation.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Great_Britain" class="extiw" title="w:Great Britain">Britain</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> dialect<span class="ib-comma">,</span> chiefly <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Yorkshire" class="extiw" title="w:Yorkshire">Yorkshire</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A maggot.</li></ol>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">now  dialectal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A corner of the mouth or eye.

<dl><dd>She considered him. A fiery droplet in the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:wick.html>wick</a></b> of her mouth considered him.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>

***wiebel.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:wiebel.html>wiebel</a> (39945)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<p>Perhaps from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">*wippelen</i>, equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wippen.html>wippen</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-elen</i>, influenced by <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">wiegelen</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">wipperen</i>, etc. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">wobble</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds">wabbeln</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">wabbeln</i>.

***wieberen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:wieberen.html>wieberen</a> (48055)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">wieberig</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zich.html>zich</a> ~ <a href = vnd.unilang:maken.html>maken</a> / ~ <a href = vnd.unilang:gaan.html>gaan</a>: (Bargoens) </i>to scarper</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en</i> lt; <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Yiddish" class="extiw" title="w:Yiddish">Yiddish</a></span> <i class="Hebr mention" lang="yi">ועייִבערעח</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="yi-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">veyiverekh</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> lt; <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hebrew_language" class="extiw" title="w:Hebrew language">Hebrew</a></span> <i class="Hebr mention" lang="he">וַיִּבְרַח</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="he-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vayivrách</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">(he) fled</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wieberen.html>wieberen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to scarper, to flee</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to leave</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to go, to move</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to move, to remove</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to lay off</li></ol>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Often used in the imperative infinitive, often with a negative charge, as in: ‘<a href = vnd.unilang:sod.html>Sod</a> off!’ Also used to indicate wavering, uncertain, amp;c. motion. Nowadays also used transitively, in which case the active <a href = vnd.unilang:perfect.html>perfect</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> formed using the auxiliary verb <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hebben.html>hebben</a></i> instead of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a></i>.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Werkwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:werkwoord.html>Werkwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:wieberen.html>wieberen</a></b>  <sup id="cite_ref-3" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-3"> | 3 | </a></sup>
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:weggaan.html>weggaan</a></li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:wied.html>wied</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">unwanted plant</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*wiod</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*weudą</i>. <p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wiel.html>wiel</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:rennen.html>rennen</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dictatoriaal.html>-er</a></i>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wielrenner.html>wielrenner</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wielrenners.html>wielrenners</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wielrenner.html>wielrennertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">wielrenster</b>)
</p>

***wiens.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:wiens.html>wiens</a> (1816)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Genitive masculine singular of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wie.html>wie</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Determiner">Determiner</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wiens.html>wiens</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">interrogative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> whose
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:wiens.html>Wiens</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:auto.html>auto</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a>?</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Whose car <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> that?</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> whose
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl">Martin <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>Van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:buren.html>Buren</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:enige.html>enige</a> Amerikaanse president <b><a href = vnd.unilang:wiens.html>wiens</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:moedertaal.html>moedertaal</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:engels.html>Engels</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>Zijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:eerste.html>eerste</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:taal.html>taal</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> Nederlands.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Martin <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>Van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:buren.html>Buren</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> the only American president whose mother tongue <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> not English. His first language <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> Dutch.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><i><a href = vnd.unilang:wiens.html>Wiens</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> come to replace its female equivalent, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wier.html>wier</a></i>, in both singular and plural. While <i><a href = vnd.unilang:wiens.html>wiens</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> the genitive masculine singular of <i><a href = vnd.unilang:wie.html>wie</a></i>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:wier.html>wier</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> the genitive feminine singular and the genitive plural. Although the use of <i><a href = vnd.unilang:wier.html>wier</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> become largely archaic and dialectal, it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> still recommended by grammarians. Example sentences of different usage:
</p>
<ul><li><a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>Hij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:enige.html>enige</a> president <i><a href = vnd.unilang:wiens.html>wiens</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:moedertaal.html>moedertaal</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:engels.html>Engels</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a>.  |  <i>He <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> the only president whose mother tongue <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> not English.</i> (genitive masculine singular)</li>
<li><a href = vnd.unilang:zij.html>Zij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:enige.html>enige</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:presidente.html>presidente</a> <i><a href = vnd.unilang:wier.html>wier</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:moedertaal.html>moedertaal</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:engels.html>Engels</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a>.  |  <i>She <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> the only president whose mother tongue <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> not English.</i> (genitive feminine singular)</li>
<li><a href = vnd.unilang:zij.html>Zij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:enige.html>enige</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:presidenten.html>presidenten</a> <i><a href = vnd.unilang:wier.html>wier</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:moedertaal.html>moedertaal</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:engels.html>Engels</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a>.  |  <i>They are the only presidents whose mother tongue <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> not English.</i> (genitive plural)</li></ul>
<hr><h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Verwante_begrippen"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:verwante.html>Verwante</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:begrippen.html>begrippen</a></i></span></h5>
<ul><li><span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">v</span>, <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">mv</span>: <a href = vnd.unilang:wier.html>wier</a></li></ul>

***wier.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:wier.html>wier</a> (12647)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:wier.html>wier</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">seaweed</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, possibly descended through Old Dutch from Proto-Germanic, or <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> borrowed from Frisian. Cognate with dialectal English <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:ware.html>ware</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">seaweed</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, Old English <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">war</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">seaweed</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:wierook.html>wierook</a> (18878)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">wierooc</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">wīrōk</i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">*wīh</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">holy</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (<span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*wīhaz</i>) + <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">rouc</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*rōk</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">smoke</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (<span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*raukiz</i>).
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wierook.html>wierook</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>incense</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wijden.html>wijden</a></span></li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:wight.html>wight</a> (52689)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href = vnd.unilang:wight.html>wight</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">wiȝt</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">wiht</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:wight.html>wight</a>, person, creature, being, <a href = vnd.unilang:whit.html>whit</a>, thing, something, anything</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*wihtiz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">essence, object</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*wekti-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">cause, sake, thing</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*wekʷ-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Scots_language" class="extiw" title="w:Scots language">Scots</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sco"><a href = German">German Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds-de"><a href = vnd.unilang:wicht.html>Wicht</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span <hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:wight.html>wight</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">wights</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A living creature, especially a human being.
<ul><li><b>circa 1602</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/William_Shakespeare" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:William Shakespeare">William Shakespeare</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikisource.org/wiki/The_Merry_Wives_of_Windsor" class="extiw" title="s:The Merry Wives of Windsor">The Merry <a href = vnd.unilang:wives.html>Wives</a> of Windsor</a></i>, act 1, scene 3:
<dl><dd><a href = vnd.unilang:o.html>O</a> base Hungarian <b><a href = vnd.unilang:wight.html>wight</a></b>! <a href = vnd.unilang:wilt.html>wilt</a> thou the spigot wield?</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1626</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/John_Milton" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:John Milton">John Milton</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikisource.org/wiki/On_the_Death_of_a_Fair_Infant_Dying_of_a_Cough" class="extiw" title="s:On the Death of a Fair Infant Dying of a Cough">On the Death of a Fair Infant Dying of a Cough</a></i>, verse vi
<dl><dd><a href = vnd.unilang:oh.html>Oh</a> say <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a> true if thou wert mortal <b><a href = vnd.unilang:wight.html>wight</a></b><br />And why from us so quickly thou didst take thy flight.</dd></dl></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1851</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Herman_Melville" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Herman Melville">Herman Melville</a>,  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Moby_Dick" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Moby Dick"><a href = vnd.unilang:moby.html>Moby</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dick.html>Dick</a></a></cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://www.gutenberg.org/ebooks/2701">[1]</a></sup>, chapter 14:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Some gamesome <b>wights</b> will tell you that they have to plant weeds there, they don’<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> grow naturally; [...]</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><b>circa 1872</b>, a <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Knight%27s_tour" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Knight | s tour">Knight's tour</a> cryptotour poem, possibly by <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Howard_Staunton" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Howard Staunton">Howard Staunton</a>, lines 1 and 2:
<dl><dd>"The <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a> that hath no love of chess/<a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>Is</a> truth to say a <a href = vnd.unilang:sorry.html>sorry</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:wight.html>wight</a></b>."</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1885</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Richard_F._Burton" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Richard F. Burton">Richard F. Burton</a>, <i>The Supplemental <a href = vnd.unilang:nights.html>Nights</a> to the Thousand <a href = vnd.unilang:nights.html>Nights</a> and a Night</i>, Night 532:
<dl><dd><span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span>Alaeddin <a href = vnd.unilang:eten.html>ate</a> and <a href = vnd.unilang:drank.html>drank</a> and <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> cheered and after he <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> rested and <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> recovered <a href = vnd.unilang:spirits.html>spirits</a> he cried, "<a href = vnd.unilang:ah.html>Ah</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:o.html>O</a> my mother, I have a sore grievance against <a href = vnd.unilang:thee.html>thee</a> for leaving <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a> to that accursed <b><a href = vnd.unilang:wight.html>wight</a></b> who strave to compass my destruction and designed to take my life. Know that I beheld Death with mine own <a href = vnd.unilang:eyes.html>eyes</a> at the hand of this damned wretch, whom thou didst certify to be my uncle;<span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span></dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">paganism</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A being of one of the Nine Worlds of Heathen belief, especially a nature spirit, <a href = vnd.unilang:elf.html>elf</a> or ancestor.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">poetic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A ghost, deity or other supernatural entity.
<ul><li><b>1789</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/William_Blake" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:William Blake">William <a href = vnd.unilang:blake.html>Blake</a></a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikisource.org/wiki/A_Dream_(Blake)" class="extiw" title="s:A Dream (Blake)">A Dream</a></i>, lines 14-16:
<dl><dd>But I saw a glow-worm near, / Who replied: ‘What wailing <b><a href = vnd.unilang:wight.html>wight</a></b> / Calls the watchman of the night?</dd></dl></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1851</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Herman_Melville" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Herman Melville">Herman Melville</a>,  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Moby_Dick" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Moby Dick"><a href = vnd.unilang:moby.html>Moby</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dick.html>Dick</a></a></cite>, chapter 2:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">“In judging of that tempestuous wind called Euroclydon,” says an old writer—of whose works I possess the only copy extant—“it maketh a marvellous difference, whether thou lookest out at it from a glass window where the frost <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> all on the outside, or whether thou observest it from that sashless window, where the frost <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> on both sides, and of which the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:wight.html>wight</a></b> Death <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> the only glazier.”</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><b>1869</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/William_Morris" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:William Morris">William Morris</a> and <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Eir%C3%ADkr_Magn%C3%BAsson" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Eiríkr Magnússon">Eiríkr Magnússon</a> (translators), <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Grettis_Saga" class="extiw" title="w:Grettis Saga">Grettis Saga: The Story of Grettir the Strong</a></i>, F. S. Ellis, page 49:
<dl><dd>Everything in their way <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> kicked out of place, the barrow-<b><a href = vnd.unilang:wight.html>wight</a></b> setting on with hideous eagerness; Grettir <a href = vnd.unilang:gave.html>gave</a> back before him for a long time, till at last it <a href = vnd.unilang:came.html>came</a> to this, that he saw it would not do to hoard his strength any more; now neither spared the other, and they <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:brought.html>brought</a> to where the horse-bones <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a>, and thereabout they wrestled long.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">fantasy</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A wraith-like creature.</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href = vnd.unilang:wight.html>wight</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse">Old <a href = vnd.unilang:norse.html>Norse</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">vígt</i>, neuter of <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">vígr</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">skilled in fighting, of age</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*wīgaz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">fighting</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*weyk-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to fight</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">wīġ</i>.<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:wight.html>wight</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic<span class="ib-comma">,</span> except in dialects</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:brave.html>Brave</a>, valorous, strong.
<ul><li><b>1485</b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:sir.html>Sir</a> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Thomas_Malory" class="extiw" title="w:Thomas Malory">Thomas Malory</a>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://quod.lib.umich.edu/c/cme/MaloryWks2/1:20.9?rgn=div2;view=fulltext">chapter ix</a>, in <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Le_Morte_d%27Arthur" class="extiw" title="w:Le Morte d | Arthur">Le <a href = vnd.unilang:morte.html>Morte</a> Darthur</a></i>, book XVIII:
<dl><dd>I haue two sones that <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> but late made knyghtes / and the eldest hyghte <a href = vnd.unilang:sir.html>sir</a> Tirre /<span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span>/ and my yongest sone hyght Lauayne / and yf hit please <a href = vnd.unilang:yow.html>yow</a> / he shalle ryde with <a href = vnd.unilang:yow.html>yow</a> vnto that Iustes / and he <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> of his age x stronge and <b>wyght</b></dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Great_Britain" class="extiw" title="w:Great Britain">Britain</a>  dialectal<span class="ib-comma">,</span> obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Strong; <a href = vnd.unilang:stout.html>stout</a>; active.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><i><abbr title="ante">a.</abbr></i> <b>1450</b>,  “<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Robin_Hood_and_the_Monk" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Robin Hood and the Monk"><a href = vnd.unilang:robin.html>Robin</a> Hood and the Monk</a>”, in Sidgwick, <a href = vnd.unilang:frank.html>Frank</a>, editor, <cite><a href="http://www.gutenberg.org/etext/28744" class="extiw" title="gutenberg:28744">Ballads of <a href = vnd.unilang:robin.html>Robin</a> Hood and other <a href = vnd.unilang:outlaws.html>Outlaws</a></a></cite>, published 1912, lines 29–34, page 98:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Then spake Much the milner son, / Ever more well him betide! / ‘Take twelve of thy <b><a href = vnd.unilang:wight.html>wight</a></b> yeomen, / Well weapon’d by thy side. / Such one would thyselfë slon, / That twelve dare not abide.’</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><i><abbr title="ante">a.</abbr></i> <b>1828</b>,  “<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Leesome_Brand" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Leesome Brand">Leesome <a href = vnd.unilang:brand.html>Brand</a></a>”, in Buchan, <a href = vnd.unilang:peter.html>Peter</a>, editor, <cite>Ancient Ballads and <a href = vnd.unilang:songs.html>Songs</a> of the North of Scotland</cite>, volume 1, published 1828, lines 21–24, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://books.google.com/books?id=KT9Odv05vMcCamp;pg=PA39">page 39</a>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Ye do you to my father's stable, / Where <a href = vnd.unilang:steeds.html>steeds</a> do stand baith <b><a href = vnd.unilang:wight.html>wight</a></b> and able; / Strike ane <a href = vnd.unilang:o.html>o</a>' them upo' the back, / The swiftest will gie his head a wap.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>
</body>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:wii.html>wii</a></b>
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:eerste.html>eerste</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:persoon.html>persoon</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:enkelvoud.html>enkelvoud</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tegenwoordige.html>tegenwoordige</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tijd.html>tijd</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> wiiën<br />
<dl><dd><ul><li><i><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:wii.html>wii</a></b>.</i> </li></ul></dd></dl></li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:wij.html>wij</a> (140)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">wi</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">wī</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*wīz</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*wéy-</i>, plural of <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*éǵh₂</i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds">wi</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">wy</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">wir</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">vi</i>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:wijden.html>wijden</a> (11221)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">wiën</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">wīen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*wīhijaną</i>. The <i>-d-</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> due to hypercorrection (<a href = vnd.unilang:regarding.html>regarding</a> the frequent loss of intervocalic <i>-d-</i>).
</p>

</p>
<ol><li>to dedicate, devote

<li>to inaugurate</li>
<li>to bless, sanctify</li></ol>

***wijdte.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:wijdte.html>wijdte</a> (71715)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:wijdde.html>wijdde</a></i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wijd.html>wijd</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-te</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***wijf.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:wijf.html>wijf</a> (2628)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:wijf.html>wijf</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">wīf</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*wībą</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wijf.html>wijf</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wijven.html>wijven</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wijfje.html>wijfje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">often derogatory</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> woman, <span class="use-with-mention">potentially being as pejorative as</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:bitch.html>bitch</a>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">Brabantian</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> Da <a href = vnd.unilang:stom.html>stom</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:wijf.html>wijf</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ij.html>ij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a> gu <a href = vnd.unilang:lige.html>lige</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gat.html>gat</a>!</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">That <a href = vnd.unilang:bitch.html>bitch</a> really <a href = vnd.unilang:took.html>took</a> advantage of <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a>!</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">often derogatory</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:babe.html>babe</a>, broad</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>The diminutive of this word <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> an independent meaning (“female animal”). Colloquial diminutives (e.g. <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">wijfie</i>) often have a familiar meaning.
</p>
