<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:wijk.html>wijk</a> (4881)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">wijc</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*wīk</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*wīkō</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">vīcus</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">village</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*weyḱ-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">village, household</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:wick.html>wick</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">-wich</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">-wick</i>, archaic <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Weich-</i> in <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Weichbild</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">municipal area</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Gothic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Gothic language">Gothic</a></span> <i class="Goth mention" lang="got">𐍅𐌴𐌹𐌷𐍃</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="got-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">weihs</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*wīhsą</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">village, settlement</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> of the same Proto-Indo-European root.
</p>

***wijl.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:wijl.html>wijl</a> (58539)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">wile</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">while</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*wīla</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hwīlō</i>.
</p><p>Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">while</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds"><a href = vnd.unilang:wiel.html>Wiel</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Weile</i>.

***wijs.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:wijs.html>wijs</a> (1752)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:wijs.html>wijs</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">wīs</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*wīsaz</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wijs.html>wijs</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wijzer.html>wijzer</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:meest.html>meest</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wijs.html>wijs</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wijst.html>wijst</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>wise</li>
<li>nice, fun (see usage notes)</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<p>Meaning 2 (nice, fun) <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> very popular in <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/East_Flanders" class="extiw" title="w:East Flanders">East Flanders</a>, in the expression <i>"<a href = vnd.unilang:vree.html>vree</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wijs.html>wijs</a>"</i>.
</p>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*wīsa</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*wīsō</i>.
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:wijzen.html>wijzen</a> (2575)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">wisen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">wīsen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*wīsijaną</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wijzen.html>wijzen</a></strong>
</p>

<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:wijs.html>Wijs</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naar.html>naar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:anderen.html>anderen</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:onbeleefd.html>onbeleefd</a>!</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Don'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> <b>point</b> at others, that's rude!</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:pijl.html>pijl</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:wijst.html>wijst</a></b> in <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:richting.html>richting</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dichtstbijzijnde.html>dichtstbijzijnde</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nooduitgang.html>nooduitgang</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The arrow <b>points</b> in the direction of the nearest emergency exit.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to point out, indicate

<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:leraar.html>leraar</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:wees.html>wees</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:leerlingen.html>leerlingen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hun.html>hun</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:fouten.html>fouten</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The teacher <b>pointed out</b> their mistakes to the students.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:wijzer.html>wijzer</a> (8141)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wijzen.html>wijzen</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dictatoriaal.html>-er</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wijzer.html>wijzer</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wijzers.html>wijzers</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wijzertje.html>wijzertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>One who points, directs, indicates</li>
<li>An arm or other moving part of an instrument which points out a readable value, notably a hand on a clock, or on another scaled dial</li></ol>

***wikken.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:wikken.html>wikken</a> (66541)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">wicken</i>, an intensive form of <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">wēgen</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to weigh</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wikken.html>wikken</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to weigh
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wegen.html>wegen</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to consider, ponder, weigh various options
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:overdenken.html>overdenken</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:overwegen.html>overwegen</a></span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<p>The sense <i>to consider</i> or <i>ponder</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> mostly used in the set phrase <i><a href = vnd.unilang:wikken.html>wikken</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wegen.html>wegen</a></i> ("to consider carefully").
</p>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>

<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wegen.html>wegen</a></span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>See the etymology of the main entry.

***wildbraad.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:wildbraad.html>wildbraad</a> (78029)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">wiltbraet</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">wiltbrāt</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">wild</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:braad.html>braad</a></i>, though note the difference in gender.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wildbraad.html>wildbraad</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>prepared game meat</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:wildbraad.html>wildbraad</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic"><a href = vnd.unilang:o.html>o</a></span>  <sup id="cite_ref-2" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-2"> | 2 | </a></sup>

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">wild</i>.

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wilde.html>wilde</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">Alternative form of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:weelde.html>weelde</a></i></span></span></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_4">Etymology 4</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">wildi</i>, a contraction of <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:wilt.html>wilt</a> gi</i> (modern <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wilt.html>wilt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gij.html>gij</a></i>).
</p>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<p>The contraction <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> sometimes reinforced with an additional <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gij.html>gij</a></i>, giving <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wilde.html>wilde</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gij.html>gij</a></i>.

***wildernis.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:wildernis.html>wildernis</a> (7311)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">wildernisse</i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:wilt.html>wilt</a></i> + <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">-nisse</i> (modern Dutch <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">wild</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-nis</i>). The <i>-r-</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> added by anology with <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hindernis.html>hindernis</a></i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:duisternis.html>duisternis</a></i>; compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Wildnis</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wildernis.html>wildernis</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wildernis.html>wildernissen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wildernis.html>wildernisje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>wilderness
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">bush</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">bush bush</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">ruigte</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:woestenij.html>woestenij</a></span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>
